Introduction To CollaboraCR2 and CollaboraCR in CR applications

This paper describes the collaborative development activities of the Apache CollaboraCR library with the purpose of presenting the data structures, management, management interface, libraries, and databases associated with a multi-year project, (2012) CollaboraCR2.2.
